<text>Ordered curbside delivery online. Order was supposed to be ready at 6:09PM. I arrived about 10 minutes early and parked in front of the store with my lights on as instructed. A lady from inside delivered to 3 different cars that were around me. She looked at me as I was watching her to hopefully let her know I was there. I sat and sat as now there were no other cars around me and I had my lights on in the middle of the front door. Finally at 6:30PM I got out of my car and walked into the restaurant.  Upon approaching I asked if my order was ready noticing that there was one order sitting in a hotbox behind the counter. A young gentleman acknowledged my order on the computer. I asked him what the point of curb side delivery was during COVID19 if I had to come inside the restaurant to get the order.  He didn't even ask what I was talking about and turned his back while saying he was sorry. The lady that made the deliveries to the other cars around me was on the phone not 5 feet away from the gentleman and when she got off the phone she definitely could hear me because she was too close to not hear me talking about my situation. < Review>
I purchased a Certified 2015 Buick Encore from Thompson's Buick GMC about 2 weeks ago now. I originally saw the car online after looking for certified cars of this make and model with low miles and good prices. I inquired online and was promptly contacted by Gary, who helped answer my questions about the car and the dealership's financing options. I wanted to finance with my personal credit union, and did not feel pressured into using the dealership's financing. In the end, my credit union wasn't able to offer me a great rate so I applied online with Thompson's and within 24 hours my application was accepted with a great first time buyer rate. Jesse called and talked me through the offer and all the additional options (extended warranty and such) and was very honest and up front about what the costs would be. I was well informed, but did not feel pressured at any point during this process. The team was willing to deliver my car to me, but since I was going out of town we ended up setting a time the following Monday for me to pick the car up at the dealership. When I got there, Gary was ready to help me test drive the car to ensure it was what I wanted. The route was a variety (a little freeway, a little hill, a little around town) so I really got a feel of how the car handled and if it was right for me. Once back inside, I worked with Eddie to go over all the final numbers (which had not changed from what I was quoted) and sign all the paperwork. Gary filled my tank with gas for free, and in about 2 hours total, I was off! I really appreciate the honesty and quality customer service I was given during this whole experience. As a young woman, I had already experienced a lot of pressure and haggling at other dealerships and I did not feel that way at Thompson's. Bonus points, the dealership is SUPER dog friendly! I had all 3 of my small dogs with me, and staff didn't even blink an eye. They were able to sit quietly with me during all the paperwork and we drove home in my new car together. Love the car I bought, and loved the experience!

For reference, my car was under $15k for a Certified 2015 with less than 20,000 miles. What a great deal!<//Review>

<Rate>5< /Rate><date>1600266762360<//date>< review>
After recently purchasing a house, we needed to have some minor electrical corrected, and several fans/control switches/can lights/dimmer switches and a stand-alone RV power outlet installed. We heard about Raceway through our realtor (who had used them for a number of years for their own properties). On the day of installation, Billy and Sam arrived on time, and were very professional and personable. Billy took our requests/needs into account for the install, and suggested very logical options that would work for the room size. We went with Billy's recommendations, and everything turned out excellent! They both worked very efficiently and answered any questions we had along the way.
Thank you guys!

A few weeks after the install, we noticed one of the fans (Brand: Minka Aire)  was making a ticking noise while operating at higher speeds. Raceway sent Sam to take a look. He figured out the problem in a few minutes, and made the correction (putting two 2" sections of gasket material 180deg apart between the ceiling and the base cover). No more ticking!!
Per the fan retailer and Raceway, this is a common issue with this brand of fans.

We intend to use Raceway for future projects.
Highly recommended!</review>

<name>Joseph Valdez< /name><time>1565071735240</time><rating>3< /rating><Review>Unremarkable atmosphere at the cost of overpriced, ordinary chicken. I had quite the appetite that afternoon. No breakfast or lunch whatsoever and I just finished with an intense workout, but even that didnt stop from reminding me how painfully average the quality and overall taste was. That's not a good sign. I ordered the california buffalo chicken burrito, not knowing what to expect except something along the lines of,  you know, meat (in this case fried chicken) and fries or potatoes- the common ingredients of any cali burrito. That is literally ALL I got. Diced wings coated LIGHTLY with sauce, and an overbearing proportion of fries wrapped in a surprisingly small package.
That may satisfy some people but for the price you pay they really couldn't think of putting one more ingredient to even out the density of the fries? It's understandable. This isnt a taco shop,  but if you have a unique, mexican inspired menu item such as this you really should get it right, or even half right. Was really disappointed, but an extreme need to feed was the reason I ate the whole thing. If I were to get it again I would definitely have dipping sauce or a side to complement it, but the price they'd charge for that I might as well go to a sit -down restaurant and pay a few buck more for such a nicer experience.< /Review>< Pictures>

<user_id>117230564611289472171< /user_id>< review>
I used the coupon from Buy1Get1. Pay $10 and get $20 worth of food. We bought the large buffalo fries to split and paid the $1.99 for extra chicken. So $12 in total for the fries. We got the pineapple jalapeno flavor. We also bought the large side of fries for $2.99 and 4 breadsticks for the kids. A regular soda as well. All that for a little over $20. The buffalo fries were enough to split between 2 hungry adults, with some left over. The taste wasn't stellar but it wasn't bad either. Wish the chicken chunks were larger. The large size of fries was huge and fed us for 3 meals. So good value there. Breadsticks were ok, but nothing to write home about. I wouldn't eat there again without a coupon, but would like to try more of their flavors. Employees were very helpful and nice.< /review>
